# Kafka Inter-Broker Replication Protocol Architecture

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the inter-broker replication protocol: the ReplicaFetcherThread, the LeaderEpochFileCache, the LogStartOffset tracking, and the ISR (in-sync replica) shrink/expand mechanism.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

Used by followers to determine correct truncation points.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java`: Reads/writes the on-disk leader epoch checkpoint file (format: version + epoch/offset entries).\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/EpochEntry.java`: Data class for a (epoch, startOffset) entry in the epoch cache.\\n\\n## LogStartOffset Tracking\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogStartOffsetIncrementReason.java`: Enum for log start offset increment reasons (LeaderOffsetIncremented, SegmentDeletion, etc.).\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java`: Contains `maybeIncrementLogStartOffset` and `maybeIncrementLocalLogStartOffset` for tracking and checkpointing the log start offset.\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/log/LogManager.scala`: Implements `checkpointLogStartOffsets` / `checkpointLogStartOffsetsInDir` to persist log start offsets to the `log-start-offset-checkpoint` file.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java`: Uses log start offset and leader epoch cache during log recovery after a broker restart.\\n- `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java`: Segment-level recovery updates the leader epoch cache.\\n\\n## ISR Shrink/Expand Mechanism\\n- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/cluster/Partition.scala`: Central ISR state machine.
